j > 0; --j) {\n        uint32_t childIndex = j - 1;\n        EventTarget* relatedTarget =\n            chain[childIndex].GetRetargetedRelatedTarget();\n        if (relatedTarget) {\n          found = true;\n          aVisitor.mEvent->mRelatedTarget = relatedTarget;\n          break;\n        }\n      }\n      if (!found) {\n        aVisitor.mEvent->mRelatedTarget =\n            aVisitor.mEvent->mOriginalRelatedTarget;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (item.HasRetargetTouchTargets()) {\n      bool found = false;\n      for (uint32_t j = i; j > 0; --j) {\n        uint32_t childIndex = j - 1;\n        if (chain[childIndex].HasRetargetTouchTargets()) {\n          found = true;\n          chain[childIndex].RetargetTouchTargets(touchEvent,\n                                                 aVisitor.mDOMEvent);\n          break;\n        }\n      }\n      if (!found) {\n        WidgetTouchEvent::TouchArray& touches = touchEvent->mTouches;\n        for (uint32_t i = 0; i < touches.Length(); ++i) {\n          touches[i]->mTarget = touches[i]->mOriginalTarget;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Target\n  aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInTargetPhase = true;\n  EventTargetChainItem& targetItem = chain[firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx];\n  // Need to explicitly retarget touch targets so that initial targets get set\n  // properly in case nothing else retargeted touches.\n  if (targetItem.HasRetargetTouchTargets()) {\n    targetItem.RetargetTouchTargets(touchEvent, aVisitor.mDOMEvent);\n  }\n  if (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped() &&\n      (!aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mNoContentDispatch ||\n       targetItem.ForceContentDispatch())) {\n    targetItem.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\n  }\n  aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInCapturePhase = false;\n  aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = true;\n  if (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped() &&\n      (!aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mNoContentDispatch ||\n       targetItem.ForceContentDispatch())) {\n    targetItem.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\n  }\n\n  if (aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInSystemGroup) {\n    targetItem.PostHandleEvent(aVisitor);\n  }\n  aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInTargetPhase = false;\n\n  // Bubble\n  for (uint32_t i = firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx + 1; i < chainLength; ++i) {\n    EventTargetChainItem& item = chain[i];\n    if (item.PreHandleEventOnly()) {\n      continue;\n    }\n    EventTarget* newTarget = item.GetNewTarget();\n    if (newTarget) {\n      // Item is at anonymous boundary. Need to retarget for the current item\n      // and for parent items.\n      aVisitor.mEvent->mTarget = newTarget;\n    }\n\n    // https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#dispatching-events\n    // Step 15.2\n    // \"Set event's relatedTarget to tuple's relatedTarget.\"\n    EventTarget* relatedTarget = item.GetRetargetedRelatedTarget();\n    if (relatedTarget) {\n      aVisitor.mEvent->mRelatedTarget = relatedTarget;\n    }\n\n    if (item.HasRetargetTouchTargets()) {\n      item.RetargetTouchTargets(touchEvent, aVisitor.mDOMEvent);\n    }\n\n    if (aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mBubbles || newTarget) {\n      if ((!aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mNoContentDispatch ||\n           item.ForceContentDispatch()) &&\n          !aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped()) {\n        item.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\n      }\n      if (aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInSystemGroup) {\n        item.PostHandleEvent(aVisitor);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = false;\n\n  if (!aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInSystemGroup &&\n      aVisitor.mEvent->IsAllowedToDispatchInSystemGroup()) {\n    // Dispatch to the system event group.  Make sure to clear the\n    // STOP_DISPATCH flag since this resets for each event group.\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mPropagationStopped = false;\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mImmediatePropagationStopped = false;\n\n    // Setting back the original target of the event.\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mTarget = aVisitor.mEvent->mOriginalTarget;\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mRelatedTarget = aVisitor.mEvent->mOriginalRelatedTarget;\n    if (firstTouchTargets) {\n      WidgetTouchEvent::TouchArray& touches = touchEvent->mTouches;\n      for (uint32_t i = 0; i < touches.Length(); ++i) {\n        touches[i]->mTarget = touches[i]->mOriginalTarget;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Special handling if PresShell (or some other caller)\n    // used a callback object.\n    if (aCallback) {\n      aCallback->HandleEvent(aVisitor);\n    }\n\n    // Retarget for system event group (which does the default handling too).\n    // Setting back the target which was used also for default event group.\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mTarget = firstTarget;\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mRelatedTarget = firstRelatedTarget;\n    if (firstTouchTargets) {\n      WidgetTouchEvent::TouchArray& touches = touchEvent->mTouches;\n      for (uint32_t i = 0; i < firstTouchTargets->Length(); ++i) {\n        touches[i]->mTarget = firstTouchTargets->ElementAt(i);\n      }\n    }\n\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInSystemGroup = true;\n    HandleEventTargetChain(aChain, aVisitor, aCallback, aCd);\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInSystemGroup = false;\n\n    // After dispatch, clear all the propagation flags so that\n    // system group listeners don't affect to the event.\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mPropagationStopped = false;\n    aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mImmediatePropagationStopped = false;\n  }\n}\n\n// There are often 2 nested event dispatches ongoing at the same time, so\n// have 2 separate caches.\nstatic const uint32_t kCachedMainThreadChainSize = 128;\nstruct CachedChains {\n  nsTArray<EventTargetChainItem> mChain1;\n  nsTArray<EventTargetChainItem> mChain2;\n};\nstatic CachedChains* sCachedMainThreadChains = nullptr;\n\n/* static */\nvoid EventDispatcher::Shutdown() {\n  delete sCachedMainThreadChains;\n  sCachedMainThreadChains = nullptr;\n}\n\nEventTargetChainItem* EventTargetChainItemForChromeTarget(\n    nsTArray<EventTargetChainItem>& aChain, nsINode* aNode,\n    EventTargetChainItem* aChild = nullptr) {\n  if (!aNode->IsInComposedDoc()) {\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n  nsPIDOMWindowInner* win = aNode->OwnerDoc()->GetInnerWindow();\n  EventTarget* piTarget = win ? win->GetParentTarget() : nullptr;\n  NS_ENSURE_TRUE(piTarget, nullptr);\n\n  EventTargetChainItem* etci = EventTargetChainItem::Create(\n      aChain, piTarget->GetTargetForEventTargetChain(), aChild);\n  if (!etci->IsValid()) {\n    EventTargetChainItem::DestroyLast(aChain, etci);\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n  return etci;\n}\n\n/* static */ EventTargetChainItem* MayRetargetToChromeIfCanNotHandleEvent(\n    nsTArray<EventTargetChainItem>& aChain, EventChainPreVisitor& aPreVisitor,\n    EventTargetChainItem* aTargetEtci, EventTargetChainItem* aChildEtci,\n    nsINode* aContent) {\n  if (!aPreVisitor.mWantsPreHandleEvent) {\n    // Keep EventTargetChainItem if we need to call PreHandleEvent on it.\n    EventTargetChainItem::DestroyLast(aChain, aTargetEtci);\n  }\n  if (aPreVisitor.mAutomaticChromeDispatch && aContent) {\n    aPreVisitor.mRelatedTargetRetargetedInCurrentScope = false;\n    // Event target couldn't handle the event. Try to propagate to chrome.\n    EventTargetChainItem* chromeTargetEtci =\n        EventTargetChainItemForChromeTarget(aChain, aContent, aChildEtci);\n    if (chromeTargetEtci) {\n      // If we propagate to chrome, need to ensure we mark\n      // EventTargetChainItem to be chrome handler so that event.composedPath()\n      // can return the right value.\n      chromeTargetEtci->SetIsChromeHandler(true);\n      chromeTargetEtci->GetEventTargetParent(aPreVisitor);\n      return chromeTargetEtci;\n    }\n  }\n  return nullptr;\n}\n\nstatic bool ShouldClearTargets(WidgetEvent* aEvent) {\n  if (auto* finalTarget = nsIContent::FromEventTargetOrNull(aEvent->mTarget)) {\n    if (finalTarget->IsInShadowTree()) {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (auto* finalRelatedTarget =\n          nsIContent::FromEventTargetOrNull(aEvent->mRelatedTarget)) {\n    if (finalRelatedTarget->IsInShadowTree()) {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n  // XXXsmaug Check also all the touch objects.\n\n  return false;\n}\n\nstatic void DescribeEventTargetForProfilerMarker(const EventTarget* aTarget,\n                                                 nsACString& aDescription) {\n  auto* node = aTarget->GetAsNode();\n  if (node) {\n    if (node->IsElement()) {\n      nsAutoString nodeDescription;\n      node->AsElement()->Describe(nodeDescription, true);\n      aDescription = NS_ConvertUTF16toUTF8(nodeDescription);\n    } else if (node->IsDocument()) {\n      aDescription.AssignLiteral(\"document\");\n    } else if (node->IsText()) {\n      aDescription.AssignLiteral(\"text\");\n    } else if (node->IsDocumentFragment()) {\n      aDescription.AssignLiteral(\"document fragment\");\n    }\n  } else if (aTarget->IsInnerWindow() || aTarget->IsOuterWindow()) {\n    aDescription.AssignLiteral(\"window\");\n  } else if (aTarget->IsRootWindow()) {\n    aDescription.AssignLiteral(\"root window\");\n  } else {\n    // Probably something that inherits from DOMEventTargetHelper.\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * https://w3c.github.io/touch-events/#cancelability\n * https://w3c.github.io/uievents/#cancelability-of-wheel-events\n */\nstatic bool IsUncancelableIfOnlyPassiveListeners(const WidgetEvent* aEvent) {\n  if (!aEvent->IsTrusted() || !aEvent->mFlags.mCancelable) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  switch (aEvent->mMessage) {\n    case eTouchStart:\n    case eTouchEnd:\n    case eTouchMove:\n    case eWheel:\n    case eLegacyMouseLineOrPageScroll:\n    case eLegacyMousePixelScroll:\n      break;\n    default:\n      return false;\n  }\n\n  // There might be non-passive listeners in the remote document\n  // So return false if we are in the parent process with remote target\n  nsCOMPtr<nsIContent> target =\n      nsIContent::FromEventTargetOrNull(aEvent->mOriginalTarget);\n  return !(XRE_IsParentProcess() && BrowserParent::GetFrom(target));\n}\n\nstruct DOMEventMarker : public BaseMarkerType<DOMEventMarker> {\n  static constexpr const char* Name = \"DOMEvent\";\n\n  using MS = MarkerSchema;\n  static constexpr MS::PayloadField PayloadFields[] = {\n      {\n          \"target\",\n          MS::InputType::CString,\n          \"Event Target\",\n          MS::Format::String,\n      },\n      {\"latency\", MS::InputType::TimeDuration, \"Latency\", MS::Format::Duration,\n       MS::PayloadFlags::None},\n      {\n          \"eventType\",\n          MS::InputType::String,\n          \"Event Type\",\n          MS::Format::String,\n      }};\n\n  static constexpr MS::Location Locations[] = {MS::Location::MarkerChart,\n                                               MS::Location::MarkerTable,\n                                               MS::Location::TimelineOverview};\n  static constexpr const char* TableLabel =\n      \"{marker.data.eventType} - {marker.data.target}\";\n  static constexpr const char* TooltipLabel =\n      \"{marker.data.eventType} - DOMEvent\";\n  static constexpr const char* ChartLabel = \"{marker.data.eventType}\";\n\n  static constexpr bool IsStackBased = true;\n\n  static void StreamJSONMarkerData(baseprofiler::SpliceableJSONWriter& aWriter,\n                                   const nsCString& aTarget,\n                                   const TimeDuration& aLatency,\n                                   const ProfilerString16View& aEventType) {\n    aWriter.StringProperty(\"eventType\", NS_ConvertUTF16toUTF8(aEventType));\n    if (!aTarget.IsEmpty()) {\n      aWriter.StringProperty(\"target\", aTarget);\n    }\n    aWriter.DoubleProperty(\"latency\", aLatency.ToMilliseconds());\n  }\n};\n\n/* static */\nnsresult EventDispatcher::Dispatch(EventTarget* aTarget,\n                                   nsPresContext* is unsafe! Fix the caller!\");\n      }\n    };\n    if (nsINode* node = nsINode::FromEventTargetOrNull(target)) {\n      // If this is a node, it's possible that this is some sort of DOM tree\n      // that is never accessed by script (for example an SVG image or XBL\n      // binding document or whatnot). \"text\": \"The Firefox DOM event dispatch chain for a click event proceeds through the following stages:\\n\\n## 1. Event Creation (Widget Layer)\\n\\nPlatform-specific widget code (e.g., `widget/gtk/nsWindow.cpp:nsWindow::OnButtonPressEvent`) creates a `WidgetMouseEvent` (defined in `widget/MouseEvents.h`) with message `eMouseDown` or `eMouseUp`, initializing it via `nsWindow::InitButtonEvent`. The event is then dispatched via `nsIWidget::DispatchInputEvent` (`widget/nsIWidget.cpp`), which may pass through the APZ (Async Pan/Zoom) layer before calling `nsIWidget::DispatchEvent`, which delivers the event to the attached `nsIWidgetListener`.\\n\\n## 2. Widget → PresShell Bridge\\n\\n`PresShellWidgetListener::HandleEvent` (`layout/base/PresShellWidgetListener.cpp`) is the concrete `nsIWidgetListener` implementation. It calls `PresShell::HandleEvent` (`layout/base/PresShell.cpp`) on the root frame.\\n\\n## 3. Event Target Identification\\n\\n`PresShell::HandleEvent` → `PresShell::EventHandler::HandleEvent` → `PresShell::EventHandler::HandleEventUsingCoordinates` performs hit-testing using `FindFrameTargetedByInputEvent` to identify the target nsIFrame at the event coordinates. `PresShell::GetEventTargetContent` / `nsIFrame::GetContentForEvent` resolve the frame to a DOM content node. The identified frame and content node are stored in `mCurrentEventTarget`.\\n\\n## 4. Pre-Dispatch Handling\\n\\n`PresShell::EventHandler::HandleEventWithCurrentEventInfo` calls `PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEvent`, which first calls `EventStateManager::PreHandleEvent` (`dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp`) to set up state, track active content, and handle pointer capture.\\n\\n## 5. DOM Event Dispatch via EventDispatcher\\n\\n`PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEventToDOM` calls `EventDispatcher::Dispatch` (`dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`) with the event target content node.\\n\\n`EventDispatcher::Dispatch` builds the **event target chain**:\\n- It creates an `EventTargetChainItem` for each target node from the event target up to the root (window), calling `EventTargetChainItem::GetEventTargetParent` → `EventTarget::GetEventTargetParent` at each step.\\n- For DOM nodes, `nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent` (`dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp`) sets `aVisitor.mParentTarget` to the parent node, building the ancestor chain.\\n- For shadow DOM, `ShadowRoot::GetEventTargetParent` (`dom/base/ShadowRoot.cpp`) handles retargeting.\\n- For the document, `Document::GetEventTargetParent` (`dom/base/Document.cpp`) continues the chain to `nsGlobalWindowInner::GetEventTargetParent`.\\n\\n## 6. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal\\n\\n`EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain` (`dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`) implements the three-phase traversal:\\n- **Capture phase**: iterates the chain from top (window) down toward the target (index high → low), calling `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent` at each item with `mFlags.mInCapturePhase = true`.\\n- **Target phase**: calls `HandleEvent` twice on the target item (once for capture listeners, once for bubble listeners) with `mFlags.mInTargetPhase = true`.\\n- **Bubble phase**: iterates from target back up to the root with `mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = true`, calling `HandleEvent` at each item (only if the event bubbles).\\n- The whole chain is then repeated for the **system event group** (`mFlags.mInSystemGroup = true`).\\n\\n## 7. Event Listener Invocation\\n\\n`EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent` calls `EventListenerManager::HandleEvent` (`dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp`), which calls `HandleEventInternal`. This:\\n- Looks up listeners by event type in the sorted `mListenerMap`.\\n- Calls `HandleEventWithListenerArray` to iterate matching listeners.\\n- For each listener matching the current phase (`Listener::MatchesEventPhase`), calls `HandleEventSingleListener`.\\n- `HandleEventSingleListener` invokes the actual listener: for WebIDL callbacks via `EventListenerHolder::GetWebIDLCallback()->HandleEvent()`; for XPCOM callbacks via `nsIDOMEventListener::HandleEvent(aDOMEvent)`.\\n- Lazily creates the DOM `Event` wrapper (e.g., `MouseEvent`) via `EventDispatcher::CreateEvent` → `NS_NewDOMMouseEvent` if not already created.\\n\\n## 8. Default Action Execution\\n\\nDefault actions are executed through two mechanisms:\\n\\na) **`ActivationBehavior`** (specified by HTML spec): After the full dispatch, `EventDispatcher::Dispatch` calls `EventTargetChainItem::ActivationBehavior` on the activation target (e.g., `HTMLInputElement::ActivationBehavior` in `dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp` or `HTMLButtonElement::ActivationBehavior` in `dom/html/HTMLButtonElement.cpp`), which submits forms, follows links, etc., unless the event was prevented.\\n\\nb) **`EventStateManager::PostHandleEvent`** (`dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp`): Called after DOM dispatch by `PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEvent`. It handles browser-level default behaviors such as dispatching click events from mouseup (via `EventStateManager::DispatchClickEvents` → `EventStateManager::InitAndDispatchClickEvent`), scrolling for wheel events, and focus changes.\\n\\nc) **`nsPresShellEventCB::HandleEvent`** (`layout/base/PresShell.cpp`): A callback passed to `EventDispatcher::Dispatch` that runs in the system event group to invoke `nsIFrame::HandleEvent` for frame-level default processing (e.g., text selection on mousedown/mouseup).\"\n}\nEOF"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":713,"cache_read_input_tokens":93803,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":713,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b73093e6-d755-491c-adac-28e9cfb29b85","uuid":"bfd1057f-fea6-4656-bd50-94beb6992b6b"}
